
## ------------ disassembly listing (8061, 1 banks) ------------


################################################################################
# 0000-00FF 8061 Internal Registers (256 Bytes)
################################################################################

#ADDR	Size	Read				Size	Write
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#0000	B/W	Zero
#0001	B/W	Zero
#0002	B	LSO port (Non-bidirectional)	B	LSO port (Non-bidirectional)
#0003	B	Bidirectional I/O port			B	Bidirectional I/O port
#0004	B	A/D Result Lo					B	A/D command (Channel #)
#0005	B	A/D Result Hi					B	Watchdog timer
#0006	W	Master I/O timer 
#0008	B	Interrupt mask					B	Interrupt mask
#0009	B	Interrupt pending				B	Interrupt pending
#000A	B	I/O status						B	I/O status
#000B	B	HSI sample register
#000C	B	HSI data mask					B	HSI data mask
#000D	B	HSI data hold					B	HSO command hold
#000E	W	HSI time hold					W	HSO time hold
#0010	B/W	Stack Pointer Lo byte			B/W	Stack Pointer Lo byte
#0011	B/W	Stack Pointer Hi byte			B/W	Stack Pointer Hi byte
#0012	B/W General purpose registers		B/W General purpose registers
#00FF	B/W General purpose registers		B/W General purpose registers

################################################################################
# 2000-2003 reset entry point
################################################################################

  reset:
2000: ff                nop                  
2001: fa                di                   disable ints;
2002: 21,6f             sjmp  2173           goto init;


################################################################################

2004: 00,00             word  0              FIXSUM                         #usually zero
2006: ff,df             word  dfff                                          #unknown; same value as A9L
2008: 00,ff             word  ff00                                          #unknown; same value as A9L
200a: bb,25             word  25bb           ROM_TO                         #checksum?
200c: 00,a0             word  a000           SMP_Base_Address               #same value as A9L
200e: 5d,00             word  5d             CC_EXECUTION_TIME              #calibration console, same value as A9L

################################################################################
# 2010-201F Interrupt Vectors
################################################################################

2010: ca,28             vect  28ca,          INT_HSO_2
2012: b6,28             vect  28b6,          INT_Timer_OVF
2014: c9,28             vect  28c9,          INT_Ignore
2016: c9,28             vect  28c9,          INT_Ignore
2018: c9,28             vect  28c9,          INT_Ignore
201a: fd,26             vect  26fd,          INT_HSO_1
201c: c9,28             vect  28c9,          INT_Ignore
201e: 9a,28             vect  289a,          INT_HSI_0

################################################################################

2020: 08                byte  8              NUM_OF_LEVELS
2021: 01                byte  1              NUM_OF_CALIBRATIONS

################################################################################
# 2022-2031 Calibration Pointers
################################################################################

2022: 90,87             word  8790           RF0
2024: 4c,8a             word  8a4c           RF2
2026: 40,8b             word  8b40           RF4
2028: 22,8d             word  8d22           RF6
202a: 64,8f             word  8f64           RF8
202c: f8,8f             word  8ff8           RFA
202e: c6,93             word  93c6           RFC
2030: a6,9c             word  9ca6           RFE

################################################################################



#### fill (=0xff) from 2032 to 20a1  ####



################################################################################
# Reset:
# 1: clear memory from 0012 - 02A0, SP is temporarily used, ends up back at 02A2 when done
#    note that we did not clear 02A2 which holds our return address (top of stack)
# 2: load initial memory state from ROM

#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
################################################################################


  setup_initial_state:
20a2: fa                di                   disable ints;                  #disable interupts, (they were already disabled, seems redundant?)
20a3: ff                nop                  
20a4: 11,0c             clrb  Rc             HSI_MASK = 0;                  #all HSI inputs disabled
20a6: a1,12,00,10       ldw   R10,12         STACK_POINTER = 12;            #temporarily point the SP at 0012; we are going to use it to clear memory
20aa: c6,11,00          stb   0,[R10++]      [STACK_POINTER++] = ZERO;      #clear current memory location and increment SP
20ad: 17,05             incb  R5             WD_TIMER++;                    #inc WD timer
20af: 3e,2a,03          jb    B6,R2a,20b5    if (!B6_VIP_mode_flag)  {      #if VIP_mode_flag (NO_START_TESTS) is set (KOEO)
20b2: 35,2a,08          jnb   B5,R2a,20bd    if (!B5_VIP_mode_flag) goto 20bd; } #and/or if VIP_mode_flag (RUNNING_TESTS) is set (KOER)
20b5: 89,2a,00,10       cmpw  R10,2a                                        #and sp points at = R2A (VIP_mode_flag)
20b9: d7,02             jne   20bd           if (STACK_POINTER == 2a)  {    #
20bb: 17,10             incb  R10            STACK_POINTER++; }             #inc SP and skip clearing VIP_mode_flag
20bd: 17,05             incb  R5             WD_TIMER++;                    #inc WD timer
20bf: 89,ec,03,10       cmpw  R10,3ec        
20c3: d3,e5             jnc   20aa           if ((uns) STACK_POINTER < 3ec) goto 20aa; #if SP less than 03EC, not finished clearing memory, else done
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
20c5: a1,36,86,14       ldw   R14,8636       R14 = 8636;                    #R14 points to first init table in rom
20c9: 89,ff,ff,14       cmpw  R14,ffff                                      #if R14 points to FFFF (no more table to process, break)
20cd: df,20             je    20ef           if (R14 == ffff) goto 20ef;    #
20cf: a2,15,1a          ldw   R1a,[R14++]    R1a = [R14++];                 #R1A is RAM offset high byte (0000), low byte is overwritten
20d2: a2,15,16          ldw   R16,[R14++]    R16 = [R14++];                 #R16 is pointer to last entry in table (contains address of next table)
20d5: 88,16,14          cmpw  R14,R16                                       #
20d8: db,0e             jc    20e8           if ((uns) R14 < R16)  {        #while we are not passed the end of table
20da: b2,15,1a          ldb   R1a,[R14++]    R1a = [R14++];                 #pointer to next byte in list
20dd: b2,1a,1c          ldb   R1c,[R1a]      R1c = [R1a];                   #store the bytes value into R1C, this value will be RAM location low byte
20e0: 92,15,1c          orb   R1c,[R14++]    R1c |= [R14++];                #the next byte is the data, or it with current value (but we've just clear
                                                                            ed mem so should have no effect?)
20e3: c6,1a,1c          stb   R1c,[R1a]      [R1a] = R1c;                   #store the value (2nd byte) into the register (1st byte)
20e6: 27,ed             sjmp  20d5           goto 20d5; }                   #contine until end of list
20e8: d9,b8             jgtu  20a2           if ((uns) R1c > [R14] ) goto setup_initial_state; #R1C should never be larger than R14, oops.
20ea: a2,16,14          ldw   R14,[R16]      R14 = [R16];                   #R14 now points at next table in ROM
20ed: 27,da             sjmp  20c9           goto 20c9;                     #continue til we've processed all init tables
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
20ef: ef,70,00          call  2162           init_RAM_pointers();
20f2: 3d,2a,06          jb    B5,R2a,20fb    if (!B5_VIP_mode_flag)  {
20f5: 3e,2a,03          jb    B6,R2a,20fb    if (!B6_VIP_mode_flag)  {
20f8: 91,01,a0          orb   Ra0,1          Ra0 |= 1; } }
20fb: a3,01,00,0d,14    ldw   R14,[d00]      R14 = [CC_PRESENT];
2100: 99,2a,15          cmpb  R15,2a         
2103: d7,12             jne   2117           if (R15 == 2a)  {
2105: a3,01,80,0c,14    ldw   R14,[c80]      R14 = [c80];
210a: 36,14,0a          jnb   B6,R14,2117    if (B6_R14)  {
210d: ad,00,30          ldzbw R30,0          R30 = (uns)0;
2110: a3,31,72,84,14    ldw   R14,[R30+8472] R14 = [R30-7b8e];
2115: 20,04             sjmp  211b           goto 211b; } }
2117: a1,22,20,14       ldw   R14,2022       R14 = RF0;
211b: a1,f0,00,18       ldw   R18,f0         R18 = f0;
211f: b3,01,20,20,1a    ldb   R1a,[2020]     R1a = [NUM_OF_LEVELS];
2124: a2,15,1c          ldw   R1c,[R14++]    R1c = [R14++];
2127: c2,19,1c          stw   R1c,[R18++]    [R18++] = R1c;
212a: e0,1a,f7          djnz  R1a,2124       R1a--;
                                             if (R1a !=  0) goto 2124;
212d: c7,be,8c,b2       stb   Rb2,[Rbe+8c]   [Rbe-74] = Rb2;
2131: ef,ca,65          call  86fe           Sub1();
2134: a3,f8,38,30       ldw   R30,[Rf8+38]   R30 = [8f9c];
2138: c3,bc,9a,30       stw   R30,[Rbc+9a]   [Rbc-66] = R30;
213c: b1,18,30          ldb   R30,18         R30 = 18;
213f: c7,01,2f,09,30    stb   R30,[92f]      [92f] = R30;
2144: 11,09             clrb  R9             INT_PEND = 0;
2146: 32,0a,06          jnb   B2,Ra,214f     if (HSI_RDY)  {
2149: b0,0d,00          ldb   0,Rd           ZERO = HSI_DATA;
214c: ff                nop                  
214d: 27,f7             sjmp  2146           goto 2146; }
214f: b0,0b,8e          ldb   R8e,Rb         R8e = HSI_SAMPLE;
2152: b1,a1,08          ldb   R8,a1          INT_MASK = a1;
2155: b1,a5,0c          ldb   Rc,a5          HSI_MASK = a5;
2158: 45,03,00,06,0e    ad3w  Re,R6,3        HSO_TIME = IO_TIMER + 3;
215d: b1,2a,0d          ldb   Rd,2a          HSO_CMD = 2a;
2160: fb                ei                   enable ints;
2161: f0                ret                  return;

  init_RAM_pointers:
2162: a1,80,01,bc       ldw   Rbc,180        Rbc = 180;
2166: a1,80,02,be       ldw   Rbe,280        Rbe = 280;
216a: a1,7c,03,a2       ldw   Ra2,37c        Ra2 = 37c;
216e: a1,6e,04,72       ldw   R72,46e        R72 = 46e;
2172: f0                ret                  return;

################################################################################
#Init: we jump here from 2000 after disabling interrupts
#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
################################################################################

  init:
2173: 11,2a             clrb  R2a            VIP_mode_flag = 0;             #clear the VIP_mode_flag; all bits
2175: a1,ee,03,10       ldw   R10,3ee        STACK_POINTER = 3ee;           #initialise stack pointer at 03EE, stack grows downwards
2179: 2f,27             scall 20a2           setup_initial_state();         #save return address to stack; interrupts enabled before returning

################################################################################
#EEC_main_loop: cycles through routines, should never terminate
#R94 - is current routine offset, will be 0 first time through
#RBC, RBE, RA2, R72 - are current RAM address pointers
#R30 - is the calculated next routine address
################################################################################

  EEC_main_loop:
217b: 99,88,94          cmpb  R94,88         
217e: db,43             jc    21c3           if ((uns) R94 >= 88) goto WATCHDOG_HANG;
2180: 9b,fd,b9,00,00    cmpb  0,[Rfc+b9]     
2185: df,2c             je    21b3           if (ZERO == [947f]) goto 21b3;
2187: 8b,fc,2a,d2       cmpw  Rd2,[Rfc+2a]   
218b: db,06             jc    2193           if ((uns) Rd2 < [93f0])  {
218d: 8b,a2,ce,06       cmpw  R6,[Ra2+ce]    
2191: db,20             jc    21b3           if ((uns) IO_TIMER >= [Ra2-32]) goto 21b3; }
2193: a0,06,42          ldw   R42,R6         R42 = IO_TIMER;
2196: 88,42,d2          cmpw  Rd2,R42        
2199: d1,0c             jleu  21a7           if ((uns) Rd2 > R42 )  {
219b: 8b,a2,ce,42       cmpw  R42,[Ra2+ce]   
219f: db,12             jc    21b3           if ((uns) R42 >= [Ra2-32]) goto 21b3;
21a1: 8b,a2,ce,d2       cmpw  Rd2,[Ra2+ce]   
21a5: d1,0c             jleu  21b3           if ((uns) Rd2 <= [Ra2-32]) goto 21b3; }
21a7: 47,fc,2a,42,d2    ad3w  Rd2,R42,[Rfc+2a] Rd2 = R42 + [93f0];
21ac: c3,a2,ce,42       stw   R42,[Ra2+ce]   [Ra2-32] = R42;
21b0: ef,7c,26          call  482f           Sub2();
21b3: ac,94,30          ldzbw R30,R94        R30 = (uns)R94;
21b6: 65,34,22,30       ad2w  R30,2234       R30 += 2234;
21ba: c9,7b,21          push  217b           push(EEC_main_loop);
21bd: ca,30             push  [R30]          push([R30]);
21bf: 75,02,94          ad2b  R94,2          R94 += 2;
21c2: f0                ret                  return;

  WATCHDOG_HANG:
21c3: fa                di                   disable ints;
21c4: ff                nop                  
21c5: 27,fc             sjmp  21c3           goto WATCHDOG_HANG;


################################################################################
#main_loop_selection: update run-mode loop selection and restart from beginning
#possible run modes are NORMAL NO_START_TESTS(KOEO) RUNNING_TESTS(KOER)
#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
#R94 - is current routine offset
################################################################################

  main_loop_selection:
21c7: c3,01,00,1f,00    stw   0,[1f00]       [1f00] = ZERO;

2203: c3,01,00,1f,00    stw   0,[1f00]       [1f00] = ZERO;

2217: b1,0f,42          ldb   R42,f          R42 = f;
221a: c7,01,ff,1f,42    stb   R42,[1fff]     [1fff] = R42;
221f: ef,40,ff          call  2162           init_RAM_pointers();           #re-init RAM pointer(s) after every function call
2222: 36,2a,04          jnb   B6,R2a,2229    if (B6_VIP_mode_flag)  {       #if VIP_mode_flag (NO_START_TESTS) is set (KOEO)
2225: b1,44,94          ldb   R94,44         R94 = 44;                      #set routine to loop B (2278; on-demand KOEO self tests)

2229: 35,2a,04          jnb   B5,R2a,2230    if (B5_VIP_mode_flag)  {       #if VIP_mode_flag (RUNNING_TESTS) is set (KOER)
222c: b1,62,94          ldb   R94,62         R94 = 62;                      #set routine to loop C (2296; on-demand KOER self tests)
222f: f0                ret                  return; }
2230: b1,00,94          ldb   R94,0          R94 = 0;                       #else set routine to loop A (2234; normal operation)
2233: f0                ret                  return;
